## Phase 2 — Encounter: The Three Gaps

### Gap 1 — Win condition unknown (HIGHEST PRIORITY)

**Before**: `@BELIEF:LAT80LON-30` held that "block inside entity2 ring at state 1 = WIN."
**After** (session 26): Route executed exactly. Block reached r40–41 c14–18 inside entity2 at state 1. Result: NOT_FINISHED.

This belief is **contradicted**. The win condition has an additional unknown requirement. You have the route geometry. You do not have the win trigger. Every session that re-executes the same 17-action route without resolving this will produce the same NOT_FINISHED.

### Gap 2 — Value-9 cluster inside entity2 (STRUCTURAL UNKNOWN)

From session 26 frame[1], rows 40–42, cols 15–17 show **value 9 inside entity2 ring** at L2 start — before the block moves there. This is not block-following trail. It was present in frame[1] and persisted through all of session 26.

Three candidates:
- **Entity1 body or leading edge** — entity1 carrier at r53–60 c1–10 has an extension that reaches into entity2
- **A target** — must be overlapped or activated to trigger WIN (analogous to how the cluster/cross triggers state advancement)
- **Structural artifact** — irrelevant to win condition

This has not been investigated at all. It is the most likely explanation for why the win condition is not firing.

### Gap 3 — Direction of entity2 entry (UNTESTED)

Block entered entity2 from above (DOWN at step 17 from r35–36 → r40–41). No session has tried entering from the LEFT (RIGHT action from c9–13 at r40–41 into c14–18), from below (UP from r45–46), or by stopping at a deeper interior row (r42–43, r44–45 instead of r40–41).

Entity2 interior spans r39–45 c13–19. The block at r40–41 is near the top of the interior. The value-9 cluster is at r40–42 c15–17 — the block at r40–41 c14–18 **does** overlap r40–41 c15–17 (3 of 5 cols). So overlap is happening. But if the win requires the block to be at r42–43 or lower (where the value-9 pattern ends), the current route stops one move too high.

---

## Phase 3 — Revise: What to Change Before Session 27

Three targeted revisions needed in the mechanics records:

### Revision A — @BELIEF:LAT80LON-30 (win condition)
Mark `contradiction_flag: true`, lower confidence to ~40. The belief that "block at r40–41 c14–18 + state 1 = WIN" is wrong. The corrected belief should read: **"block inside entity2 at state 1 is necessary but not sufficient; additional condition unknown."** See @BELIEF:LAT50LON-30 for hypothesis ranking.
